			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">Net sales of maintenance products, which are considered the primary growth focus for the Company, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">de</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">creased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">3 percent</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> in the first quarter when compared to the prior </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">year fiscal quarter.&nbsp; </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">This </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">de</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">crease was d</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">ue</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> primarily </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">to lower </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">sales of WD-40 Multi-Use Product </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">with</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">Asia</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">-</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">Pacific</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> segment</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">.&nbsp; </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> of homecare and cleaning products </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">in</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">creased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">1 percent</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> the first quarter compared to the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">prior </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">year fiscal quarter.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Many of the Company&#x2019;s homecare and cleaning products, particularly those in the U.S., are considered harvest brands providing healthy profit returns to the Company but are becoming a smaller part of the business as net sales of maintenance products grow </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">in line with</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> the execution of the Co</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">mpany&#x2019;s strategic initiatives</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.&nbsp; </font></p></td></tr></table></div>

Other forward-looking and material information may also be discussed during this call.&nbsp; </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Please visit </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;text-decoration:underline;color:#000000;">http://investor.wd40company.com</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> for more information and to view</font><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">supporting materials.&nbsp;</font>

		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About WD-40 Company</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40 Company is a global marketing organization dedicated to creating positive lasting memories by developing and selling products that solve problems in workshops, factories and homes around the world. The Company markets its maintenance products and homecare and cleaning products under the following well-known brands: WD-40&#xAE;, 3-IN-ONE&#xAE;, GT85&#xAE;, X-14&#xAE;, 2000 Flushes&#xAE;, Carpet Fresh&#xAE;, no vac&#xAE;, Spot Shot&#xAE;, 1001&#xAE;,&nbsp;Lava&#xAE;</font><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">and Solvol&#xAE;. &nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Headquartered in San Diego, WD-40 Company recorded net sales of $423.4 million in fiscal year 2019 and its products are currently available in more than 176 countries and territories worldwide. WD-40 Company is traded on the NASDAQ Global Select market under the ticker symbol &#x201C;WDFC.&#x201D; For additional information about WD-40 Company please visit</font><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;text-decoration:underline;color:#000000;">http://www.wd40company.com</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font>
